## TOPIC 00002: Arb

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb.html`

- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: GroupsAdvancedData TransferPulse ShapingWaveform AttributesWaveform CapabilitiesWrite Waveform Burst DetectionGroup membersNameDescriptionNIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_CARRIER_FREQUENCYIndicates the carrier frequency generated by the arbitrary waveform generator (AWG) module. NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_POWERIndicates the av

### Arb

#### Groups

- Advanced
- Data Transfer
- Pulse Shaping
- Waveform Attributes
- Waveform Capabilities
- Write Waveform Burst Detection

#### Group members

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_CARRIER_FREQUENCY | Indicates the carrier frequency generated by the arbitrary waveform generator (AWG) module. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_POWER | Indicates the average output power from the PXI-5421, PXI-5441, PXIe-5442, and PXIe-5450 AWG module. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_PRE_FILTER_GAIN | Specifies the AWG prefilter gain. The prefilter gain is applied to the waveform data before any other signal processing. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_REPEAT_COUNT | Specifies the repeat count of a waveform when you set the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_REPEAT_COUNT_IS_FINITE attribute to VI_TRUE. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_REPEAT_COUNT_IS_FINITE | Specifies the repetition mode of a waveform when you set the NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE attribute to NIRFSG_VAL_ARB_WAVEFORM. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_SOFTWARE_SCALING_FACTOR | Specifies how much to scale the data before writing it with the niRFSG_WriteArbWaveform function. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_DEVICE_INSTANTANEOUS_BANDWIDTH | Specifies the bandwidth of the device. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_EQUALIZATION_ENABLED | When this attribute is enabled, NI-RFSG equalizes the waveform data to correct for variations in the response of the NI-RFSG device. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_PATTERN | Enables or disables digital pattern on the PXI-5421/5441 AWG module. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE | Specifies whether to generate a continuous wave (CW) signal, the arbitrary waveform specified by the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_SELECTED_WAVEFORM attribute, or the script specified by the NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT attribute, upon calling the niRFSG_Initiate function. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATE | This attribute specifies the I/Q rate of the arbitrary waveform. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_SWAP_ENABLED | Enables or disables the inverse phase rotation of the I/Q signal by swapping the I and Q inputs. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_MEMORY_SIZE | The total amount of memory on the signal generator in bytes. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_PHASE_CONTINUITY_ENABLED | Specifies whether the driver maintains phase continuity in the arbitrary waveforms. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT | Specifies the script in onboard memory to generate upon calling the niRFSG_Initiate function when the NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE attribute is set to NIRFSG_VAL_SCRIPT. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_SIGNAL_BANDWIDTH | Specifies the bandwidth of the arbitrary signal. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_WRITE_WAVEFORM_NORMALIZATION | Specifies whether to perform the normalization on a waveform. |

#### Attachments

None

Parent topic:

Attributes

## TOPIC 00003: NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATE

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga218a1b75e8eb2d4026526b9f756c3bbf.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga218a1b75e8eb2d4026526b9f756c3bbf.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: This attribute specifies the I/Q rate of the arbitrary waveform. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATENumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1250452ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks The I/Q rate is coerced to a value the hardware can achieve. Read this value back after setting it to see the actual I/Q rate. NI-RFSG i

### NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATE

This attribute specifies the I/Q rate of the arbitrary waveform.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATE

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1250452 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

f

f

NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE

NIRFSG_VAL_ARB_WAVEFORM

NIRFSG_VAL_SCRIPT

Note

Use this attribute to associate an I/Q rate with a waveform.

**Valid Values:**

| Device | I/Q Rates |
| --- | --- |
| PXIe-5644/5645 | Up to 120 MS/s. |
| PXIe-5646 | Up to 250 MS/s. |
| PXI-5670 | 50 MS/s* 100 MS/s |
| PXI-5671 | 50 MS/s* 100 MS/s *(100 MS/s)/*_n_, where n is divisible by 2 between 12 to 512, and divisible by 4 between 512 to 1,024 (n = 12, 14, 16, ..., 512, 516, 520, ..., 1,024). Setting the I/Q rate to one of these values enables the DUC. |
| PXIe-5672 | Up to 100 MS/s. |
| PXIe-5673/5673E | Up to 200 MS/s.Note If a PXIe-5450 with module revisions A or B is used as part of your PXIe-5673/5673E, the NI-FGEN NIFGEN_ATTR_COMPENSATE_FOR_FILTER_GROUP_DELAY attribute is disabled if the requested I/Q rate is less than 1.5 MS/s. |
| PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5860 | Up to 1.25 GS/s. |
| PXI-5842 (500 MHz, 1 GHz, and 2 GHz bandwidth options) | Up to 2.5 GS/s. |
| PXIe-5842 (4 GHz bandwidth option) using the Standard personality | Up to 2.5 GS/s. |
| PXIe-5842 (4 GHz bandwidth option) using the 4 GHz Bandwidth personality | 5 GS/s only. |

- NI-RFSG is forced to place the carrier frequency at 18 MHz ± 1 MHz to avoid aliasing. This means that NI-RFSG cannot select a carrier frequency that could optimize waveform size if phase continuity is enabled.
- Output signal bandwidth must be <5 MHz to avoid aliasing.
- Close-in phase noise is higher.

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Streaming](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/streaming.html)

[Assigning Properties or Attributes to a Waveform](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/assigning-properties-or-attributes-to-a-wavef.html)–Refer to this topic for more information about using this attribute to associate an I/Q rate with a waveform.

[Digital Upconverter](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/digital-upconverter.html)

Parent topic:

Arb

## TOPIC 00004: NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_SWAP_ENABLED

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga286ea05f2d588cc50e27294aa7464c9f.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga286ea05f2d588cc50e27294aa7464c9f.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Enables or disables the inverse phase rotation of the I/Q signal by swapping the I and Q inputs. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_SWAP_ENABLEDNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1250404ViBooleanRead/WriteN/ARemarks To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.Defined Values:Val

### NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_SWAP_ENABLED

Enables or disables the inverse phase rotation of the I/Q signal by swapping the I and Q inputs.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_SWAP_ENABLED

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1250404 | ViBoolean | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

**Defined Values:**

| Value | Description |
| --- | --- |
| VI_TRUE | NI-RFSG device applies noninverse phase rotation of the I/Q signal. |
| VI_FALSE | NI-RFSG device applies inverse phase rotation of the I/Q signal. |

**Default Value:** VI_FALSE

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_REPEAT_COUNT

Specifies the repeat count of a waveform when you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_REPEAT_COUNT_IS_FINITE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gac72448da5d60440ec0cb6722ffa7343f.html) attribute to VI_TRUE.

## TOPIC 00006: NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_PRE_FILTER_GAIN

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga466494676d3fb94fc73f43c9ebd227d9.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga466494676d3fb94fc73f43c9ebd227d9.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the AWG prefilter gain. The prefilter gain is applied to the waveform data before any other signal processing. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_PRE_FILTER_GAINNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150025ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks Reduce this value to prevent overflow in the AWG interpolation filte

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_PRE_FILTER_GAIN

Specifies the AWG prefilter gain. The prefilter gain is applied to the waveform data before any other signal processing.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_PRE_FILTER_GAIN

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150025 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

Reduce this value to prevent overflow in the AWG interpolation filters. Other gains on the NI-RFSG device are automatically adjusted to compensate for nonunity AWG prefilter gain. The PXI-5671, PXIe-5672 must be in the Configuration state to use this attribute. However, the PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5673/5673E, and PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842 can be in either the Configuration or the Generation state to use this attribute. PXIe-5860 can only be in the Configuration state to use this attribute.

On the PXI-5671, this attribute applies only when the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga218a1b75e8eb2d4026526b9f756c3bbf.html) attribute is set to a value less than or equal to 8.33MS/s. On the PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, and PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860, this attribute is always applicable.

**Units**: dB

**Default Value:** 0dB

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

Parent topic:

Arb

## TOPIC 00007: NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_CARRIER_FREQUENCY

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga7a7ccd0c5bea2e0a54513e2fa7e83d10.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga7a7ccd0c5bea2e0a54513e2fa7e83d10.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Indicates the carrier frequency generated by the arbitrary waveform generator (AWG) module. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_CARRIER_FREQUENCYNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150015ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks The specified carrier frequency is related to the RF output as shown in the following equations

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_CARRIER_FREQUENCY

Indicates the carrier frequency generated by the arbitrary waveform generator (AWG) module.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_CARRIER_FREQUENCY

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150015 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The specified carrier frequency is related to the RF output as shown in the following equations:

| Device | Equation |
| --- | --- |
| PXI-5610, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672 | RF Frequency (MHz) = Upconverter Center Frequency + Arb Carrier Frequency – 25 MHz |
| PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5673/5673E, PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860 | RF Frequency (MHz) = Upconverter Center Frequency + Arb Carrier FrequencyNote The NIRFSG_ATTR_UPCONVERTER_CENTER_FREQUENCY attribute and the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_CARRIER_FREQUENCY attribute cannot be set at the same time. The only time the carrier frequency is nonzero on these devices is when in-band retuning is used. |

Note

Use this attribute to associate a carrier frequency with a waveform.

Note

This attribute is read-only on the PXI-5670/5671 and PXIe-5672.

**Units**: hertz (Hz)

**Supported Devices:** PXI-5610, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Assigning Properties or Attributes to a Waveform](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/assigning-properties-or-attributes-to-a-wavef.html)–Refer to this topic for more information about using this attribute to associate a carrier frequency with a waveform.

Parent topic:

Arb

## TOPIC 00008: NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_POWER

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga869be4bba8675f882bf1ffe202668d7f.html

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Indicates the average output power from the PXI-5421, PXI-5441, PXIe-5442, and PXIe-5450 AWG module. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_POWERNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150016ViReal64Read-OnlyN/ARemarks If an arbitrary waveform is being generated, this attribute specifies either the average power or t

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_POWER

Indicates the average output power from the PXI-5421, PXI-5441, PXIe-5442, and PXIe-5450 AWG module.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_POWER

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150016 | ViReal64 | Read-Only | N/A |

#### Remarks

If an arbitrary waveform is being generated, this attribute specifies either the average power or the peak power of the signal, depending on the [NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL_TYPE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga57126bb84c21a6b74bc19a7f07e1ff18.html) attribute setting.

**Units**: dBm

**Supported Devices:** PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E

## TOPIC 00009: NIRFSG_ATTR_WRITE_WAVEFORM_NORMALIZATION

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga86c8238af79b82ec4dd3aff41690edaf.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga86c8238af79b82ec4dd3aff41690edaf.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to perform the normalization on a waveform. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_WRITE_WAVEFORM_NORMALIZATIONNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150293ViInt32Read/WriteN/ARemarksYou can not set NIRFSG_ATTR_WRITE_WAVEFORM_NORMALIZATION and NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL_TYPE attributes at the same time.De

### NIRFSG_ATTR_WRITE_WAVEFORM_NORMALIZATION

Specifies whether to perform the normalization on a waveform.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_WRITE_WAVEFORM_NORMALIZATION

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150293 | ViInt32 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

Note

You can not set [NIRFSG_ATTR_WRITE_WAVEFORM_NORMALIZATION](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga86c8238af79b82ec4dd3aff41690edaf.html) and [NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL_TYPE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga57126bb84c21a6b74bc19a7f07e1ff18.html) attributes at the same time.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_DISABLE | 0 (0x0) | Disables normalization on the waveform. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_ENABLE | 1 (0x1) | Enables normalization on a waveform to transform the waveform data so that its maximum is 1.00 and its minimum is -1.00 |

**Default Value:****NIRFSG_VAL_DISABLE**

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

Parent topic:

Arb

## TOPIC 00010: NIRFSG_ATTR_MEMORY_SIZE

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga977285b25bf6bbbd0ac2abced2b1a92f.html

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: The total amount of memory on the signal generator in bytes. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_MEMORY_SIZENumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150061ViInt64Read-OnlyN/ARemarksNot all onboard memory is available for waveform storage. A portion of onboard memory stores scripts that specify how the waveforms are gen

### NIRFSG_ATTR_MEMORY_SIZE

The total amount of memory on the signal generator in bytes.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_MEMORY_SIZE

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150061 | ViInt64 | Read-Only | N/A |

#### Remarks

Note

Not all onboard memory is available for waveform storage. A portion of onboard memory stores scripts that specify how the waveforms are generated. These scripts typically require less than 1KB of onboard memory.

**Units:** bytes

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Memory Options](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/memory-options.html)

[Phase Continuity](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/pxi-5670-features/page/phase-continuity.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00011: NIRFSG_ATTR_DEVICE_INSTANTANEOUS_BANDWIDTH

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga97faedf941a4826a8ff6a7bbcadcd9c0.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga97faedf941a4826a8ff6a7bbcadcd9c0.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the bandwidth of the device. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_DEVICE_INSTANTANEOUS_BANDWIDTHNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150226ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks The instantaneous bandwidth is the effective real-time bandwidth of the signal path for your configuration.The NIRFSG_ATTR_SIGNAL_BANDWIDTH

### NIRFSG_ATTR_DEVICE_INSTANTANEOUS_BANDWIDTH

Specifies the bandwidth of the device.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_DEVICE_INSTANTANEOUS_BANDWIDTH

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150226 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The instantaneous bandwidth is the effective real-time bandwidth of the signal path for your configuration.

The [NIRFSG_ATTR_SIGNAL_BANDWIDTH](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gabf8c34b562dc44865eafb7925d39c6d7.html), centered at the NIRFSG_ATTR_FREQUENCYmust fit within the device instantaneous bandwidth, which is centered at the [NIRFSG_ATTR_UPCONVERTER_CENTER_FREQUENCY](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf__upconverter_1gaab3d8456582e073b17cc19a383374962.html).

**Units**: Hz

**Default Value**: N/A

**Supported Devices**: PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[PXIe-5830 Frequency and Bandwidth Selection](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/pxie-5830-feature/page/frequency-and-bandwidth-selection.html)

[PXIe-5831/5832 Frequency and Bandwidth Selection](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/pxie-5831/page/frequency-and-bandwidth-selection.html)

[PXIe-5841 Frequency and Bandwidth Selection](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/pxie-5841/page/frequency-and-bandwidth-selection.html)

## TOPIC 00012: NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gae0a986dda1374495d678eda99ae48e00.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gae0a986dda1374495d678eda99ae48e00.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the script in onboard memory to generate upon calling the niRFSG_Initiate function when the NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE attribute is set to NIRFSG_VAL_SCRIPT. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPTNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150023ViStringRead/WriteN/ARemarks The NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED

### NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT

Specifies the script in onboard memory to generate upon calling the [niRFSG_Initiate](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions_1ga31ed10584ebd85f37876b131d6a36335.html) function when the [NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaeeb484671453f0db6a049395402aba67.html) attribute is set to **NIRFSG_VAL_SCRIPT**.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150023 | ViString | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The [NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gae0a986dda1374495d678eda99ae48e00.html) attribute is ignored when the [NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaeeb484671453f0db6a049395402aba67.html) attribute is set to **NIRFSG_VAL_ARB_WAVEFORM** or **NIRFSG_VAL_CW**. To set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gae0a986dda1374495d678eda99ae48e00.html) attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Assigning Properties or Attributes to a Waveform](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/assigning-properties-or-attributes-to-a-wavef.html)

[Scripting Instructions](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/scripting-instructions.html)

Parent topic:

Arb

## TOPIC 00013: NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaeeb484671453f0db6a049395402aba67.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaeeb484671453f0db6a049395402aba67.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to generate a continuous wave (CW) signal, the arbitrary waveform specified by the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_SELECTED_WAVEFORM attribute, or the script specified by the NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT attribute, upon calling the niRFSG_Initiate function. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODENumeric

### NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE

Specifies whether to generate a continuous wave (CW) signal, the arbitrary waveform specified by the [NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_SELECTED_WAVEFORM](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__waveform__capabilities_1gacc49d770986f2104f72c010917595eab.html) attribute, or the script specified by the [NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gae0a986dda1374495d678eda99ae48e00.html) attribute, upon calling the [niRFSG_Initiate](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions_1ga31ed10584ebd85f37876b131d6a36335.html) function.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150018 | ViInt32 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_ARB_WAVEFORM | 1001 (0x3e9) | Configures the RF signal generator to generate the arbitrary waveform specified by the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_SELECTED_WAVEFORM attribute. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_CW | 1000 (0x3e8) | Configures the RF signal generator to generate a CW signal. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_SCRIPT | 1002 (0x3ea) | Configures the RF signal generator to generate arbitrary waveforms as directed by the NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT attribute. |

**Default Value:****NIRFSG_VAL_CW**

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696 (CW support only), PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/assigning-properties-or-attributes-to-a-wavef.html](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/assigning-properties-or-attributes-to-a-wavef.html)

[Scripting Instructions](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/scripting-instructions.html)–Refer to this topic for more information about scripting.

**High-Level Functions**:

- [niRFSG_ConfigureGenerationMode](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__configure__waveform_1ga7b0515c71bce7bebe6c57204cb5539bf.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00014: NIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_EQUALIZATION_ENABLED

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaefd72c080666f84afbf4d1d1b37ea4e4.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaefd72c080666f84afbf4d1d1b37ea4e4.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: When this attribute is enabled, NI-RFSG equalizes the waveform data to correct for variations in the response of the NI-RFSG device. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_EQUALIZATION_ENABLEDNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150012ViInt32Read/WriteN/ARemarks Enabling digital equalization improves the modul

### NIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_EQUALIZATION_ENABLED

When this attribute is enabled, NI-RFSG equalizes the waveform data to correct for variations in the response of the NI-RFSG device.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_EQUALIZATION_ENABLED

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150012 | ViInt32 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

Enabling digital equalization improves the modulation error rates (MER) and error vector magnitude (EVM) for signals with large bandwidths (>500 kHz), but it increases tuning times.

On the PXI-5670/5671, equalization is performed in the software, so tuning time is increased. On the PXIe-5672, equalization is performed in the hardware so that there is no compromise in performance.

This attribute applies only when the [NIRFSG_ATTR_GENERATION_MODE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaeeb484671453f0db6a049395402aba67.html) attribute is set to **NIRFSG_VAL_ARB_WAVEFORM** or **NIRFSG_VAL_SCRIPT**. To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860: **NIRFSG_VAL_ENABLE** is the only supported value for this device.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_DISABLE | 0 (0x0) | Filter is not applied |
| NIRFSG_VAL_ENABLE | 1 (0x1) | Filter is applied. |

**Default Value:**

PXI-5670/5671: **NIRFSG_VAL_DISABLE**

PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5672, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860: **NIRFSG_VAL_ENABLE**

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Response and Software Equalization](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/response-and-software-equalization.html)–Refer to this topic for more information about equalization performed in software.

[Frequency Tuning Times](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/frequency-tuning-times.html)

Parent topic:

Arb

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaefe3eb3cddfbcf76a49bff21e2283163.html language=enus -->

## TOPIC 00017: NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_DIGITAL_GAIN

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__advanced_1ga3f69d99da351c9c7466a7970ad05a53f.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__advanced_1ga3f69d99da351c9c7466a7970ad05a53f.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the digital gain, in decibels. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_DIGITAL_GAINNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150204ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks The digital gain is applied to the waveform data after filtering. Use this attribute to adjust the output power of the device while keeping the analog

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_DIGITAL_GAIN

Specifies the digital gain, in decibels.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_DIGITAL_GAIN

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150204 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The digital gain is applied to the waveform data after filtering. Use this attribute to adjust the output power of the device while keeping the analog path fixed. This may cause clipping, overflows, or quantization noise if used improperly.

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration or Generation state.

**Default Value:** 0 dB

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

Parent topic:

Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__advanced_1ga63c6de35d9613d4f5319ca58bbfc831c.html language=enus -->

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

### NIRFSG_ATTR_OVERFLOW_ERROR_REPORTING

Configures error reporting for onboard signal processing (OSP) overflows.

NIRFSG_ATTR_OVERFLOW_ERROR_REPORTING

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |

Overflows lead to clipping of the waveform.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_ERROR_REPORTING_DISABLED | 1302 (0x516) | NI-RFSG does not return an error or a warning when an OSP overflow occurs. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_ERROR_REPORTING_WARNING | 1301 (0x515) | NI-RFSG returns a warning when an OSP overflow occurs. |

## TOPIC 00019: NIRFSG_ATTR_COMPENSATE_FOR_FILTER_GROUP_DELAY

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__advanced_1gabc8ec4365a67a273bf15a15b90853496.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__advanced_1gabc8ec4365a67a273bf15a15b90853496.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Enables or disables compensation for filter group delay on the AWG module. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_COMPENSATE_FOR_FILTER_GROUP_DELAYNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1152832ViBooleanRead/WriteN/ARemarks This attribute also accounts for the upconverter group delay and aligns the RF output with the Star

### NIRFSG_ATTR_COMPENSATE_FOR_FILTER_GROUP_DELAY

Enables or disables compensation for filter group delay on the AWG module.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_COMPENSATE_FOR_FILTER_GROUP_DELAY

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1152832 | ViBoolean | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

This attribute also accounts for the upconverter group delay and aligns the RF output with the Started Event, Done Event, and Marker Events.

At a low I/Q rate, the group delay can become so large that some devices may not be able to align the events with the RF output, in which case you must increase the I/Q rate or disable this attribute.

**Defined Values:**

| Value | Description |
| --- | --- |
| VI_TRUE | Enables compensation for filter group delay. |
| VI_FALSE | Disables compensation for filter group delay. |

**Default Value:** VI_FALSE

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5672

Parent topic:

Advanced

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__data__transfer_1ga3838f11f122524b746965ff087e655a5.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00022: NIRFSG_ATTR_DIRECT_DOWNLOAD

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__data__transfer_1ga3838f11f122524b746965ff087e655a5.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__data__transfer_1ga3838f11f122524b746965ff087e655a5.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether the niRFSG_WriteArbWaveform function immediately writes waveforms to the device or copies the waveform to host memory for later download. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_DIRECT_DOWNLOADNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150042ViInt32Read/WriteN/ARemarks NI-RFSG reads and validates this attri

### NIRFSG_ATTR_DIRECT_DOWNLOAD

Specifies whether the [niRFSG_WriteArbWaveform](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__configure__waveform_1ga80c6476b14d33dbc57930b85cba7f9e5.html) function immediately writes waveforms to the device or copies the waveform to host memory for later download.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_DIRECT_DOWNLOAD

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150042 | ViInt32 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

NI-RFSG reads and validates this attribute when an arbitrary waveform is first allocated.

For the PXI-5670, direct download is always disabled. For all other devices, direct download is always enabled.

PXI-5671: To increase performance when using large waveforms, enable direct download. To maximize reconfigurability, disable direct download.

Perform the following steps to enable direct download:

1. Set the I/Q rate to less than or equal to 8.33MS/s with the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga218a1b75e8eb2d4026526b9f756c3bbf.html) attribute.

2. Set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL_TYPE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga57126bb84c21a6b74bc19a7f07e1ff18.html) attribute to **NIRFSG_VAL_PEAK_POWER**.

3. Disable the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_SWAP_ENABLED](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga286ea05f2d588cc50e27294aa7464c9f.html) attribute.

4. Disable the [NIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_EQUALIZATION_ENABLED](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1gaefd72c080666f84afbf4d1d1b37ea4e4.html) attribute.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_DISABLE | 0 (0x0) | The RF In local oscillator signal is not present at the front panel LO OUT connector. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_ENABLE | 1 (0x1) | The RF In local oscillator signal is present at the front panel LO OUT connector. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_UNSPECIFIED | -2 (-0x2) | The RF IN local oscillator signal may or may not be present at the front panel LO OUT connector, because NI-RFSA may be controlling it. |

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5840/5841/5842/5860

Parent topic:

Data Transfer

## TOPIC 00029: NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_SIZE_MAX

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__waveform__capabilities_1gaeb5a8094d76f798ecc35c1ce895d150e.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb__waveform__capabilities_1gaeb5a8094d76f798ecc35c1ce895d150e.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Returns the size of the largest waveform that is allowed. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_SIZE_MAXNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1250457ViInt32Read-OnlyN/ARemarks To read this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.For the PXI-5671 and PXIe-5672, the value of this att

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_SIZE_MAX

Returns the size of the largest waveform that is allowed.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_SIZE_MAX

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1250457 | ViInt32 | Read-Only | N/A |

#### Remarks

To read this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

For the PXI-5671 and PXIe-5672, the value of this attribute depends on the I/Q rate. Set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_RATE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__arb_1ga218a1b75e8eb2d4026526b9f756c3bbf.html) before reading this attribute. For the PXIe-5673/5673E, the maximum waveform size is reduced to account for the amount of device memory currently used.

Note

Not all onboard memory is available for waveform storage. A portion of onboard memory stores scripts that specify how the waveforms are generated. These scripts typically require less than 1KB of onboard memory.

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**High-Level Functions**:

- [niRFSG_QueryArbWaveformCapabilities](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gacd105a094729b1ac2a622705777e4353.html)

Parent topic:

Waveform Capabilities

### NIRFSG_ATTR_EXPORTED_REF_CLOCK_OUTPUT_TERMINAL

Specifies the destination terminal for exporting the Reference Clock on the RF signal generators.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_EXPORTED_REF_CLOCK_OUTPUT_TERMINAL

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150053 | ViString | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_CLK_OUT_STR | ClkOut | Exports the Reference Clock signal to the CLK OUT connector of the device. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_DO_NOT_EXPORT_STR |  | The Reference Clock signal is not exported. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_REF_OUT_STR | RefOut | Exports the Reference Clock signal to the REF OUT connector of the device. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_REF_OUT2_STR | RefOut2 | Exports the Reference Clock signal to the REF OUT2 connector of the device, if applicable. |

**Default Value:****NIRFSG_VAL_DO_NOT_EXPORT_STR**

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXIe-5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

| Defined Output Terminal Values | Supported on PXIe-5644/5645/5646,PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860 | Supported on PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/56521 | Supported on PXIe-5653 | Supported on PXIe-5654, PXIe-5654 with PXIe-5696 | Supported on PXIe-5673 | Supported on PXIe-5673E |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_REF_OUT_STR | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |
| NIRFSG_VAL_REF_OUT2_STR | No | Yes | No | Yes | No | Yes |
| NIRFSG_VAL_CLK_OUT_STR | No | No | No | No | Yes | Yes |
| NIRFSG_VAL_DO_NOT_EXPORT_STR | Yes | Yes | No | Yes | Yes | Yes |

<sup>1</sup>The **NIRFSG_VAL_REF_OUT2_STR** output terminal value is valid for only the PXIe-5650/5651/5652, not the PXI-5650/5651/5652.

**Related Topics**

## TOPIC 00032: NIRFSG_ATTR_ACTIVE_CONFIGURATION_LIST

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__configuration__list_1ga30dd8bcb8d4424caeada45ac08d2acd6.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__configuration__list_1ga30dd8bcb8d4424caeada45ac08d2acd6.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the name of the configuration list to make active. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ACTIVE_CONFIGURATION_LISTNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150096ViStringRead/WriteN/ARemarks When you get or set an attribute and it is in the configuration list configuration, the attribute is set to or read from t

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ACTIVE_CONFIGURATION_LIST

Specifies the name of the configuration list to make active.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ACTIVE_CONFIGURATION_LIST

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150096 | ViString | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

When you get or set an attribute and it is in the configuration list configuration, the attribute is set to or read from the active list step of the active configuration list.

If the [NIRFSG_ATTR_ACTIVE_CONFIGURATION_LIST](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__configuration__list_1ga30dd8bcb8d4424caeada45ac08d2acd6.html) attribute is set to "" (empty string), no list is active.

Note

For the PXIe-5650/5651/5652 and PXIe-5673E, when this attribute is set to a valid list name, the [NIRFSG_ATTR_FREQUENCY_SETTLING_UNITS](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga70ee5ae4ef92a49366c7f070f769377d.html) attribute supports only **NIRFSG_VAL_TIME_AFTER_IO** as a valid value.

**Default Value:** ""

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXIe-5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860, PXIe-5842 with S-parameters, PXIe-5842 with 54GHz Frequency Extension, PXIe-5860 with S-parameters

**Related Topics**

[RF List Mode](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/rf-list-mode.html)

[Using RF List Mode](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/using-rf-list-mode.html)

## TOPIC 00043: NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_COMMON_MODE_OFFSET

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga280afdde1059fd2f5c1d83778574c0bc.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga280afdde1059fd2f5c1d83778574c0bc.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the common-mode offset applied to the signals generated at each differential output terminal. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_COMMON_MODE_OFFSETNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150148ViReal64Read/WriteChannelsRemarks This attribute applies only when you set the NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_

### NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_COMMON_MODE_OFFSET

Specifies the common-mode offset applied to the signals generated at each differential output terminal.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_COMMON_MODE_OFFSET

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150148 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | Channels |

#### Remarks

This attribute applies only when you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_TERMINAL_CONFIGURATION](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga9a3ee859b6e753e1ac1b2042ef1aed9b.html) attribute to **NIRFSG_VAL_DIFFERENTIAL**. Common-mode offset shifts both positive and negative terminals in the same direction.

To use this attribute, you must use the channelName parameter of the [niRFSG_SetAttributeViReal64](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1gae1e8e18281fe5567a905907fff0c7a93.html) function to specify the name of the channel you are configuring. For the PXIe-5645, you can configure the I and Q channels by using I or Q as the channel string, or set the channel string to "" (empty string) to configure both channels. For the PXIe-5820, the only valid value for the channel string is "" (empty string).

Note

For the PXIe-5645, this attribute is ignored if you are using the RF ports.

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

**Units:** Volts

**Valid Values:**

PXIe-5645: -0.8V to 0.8V if you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_LOAD_IMPEDANCE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga0ba856adbe0079fec19cc81088b5cc88.html) attribute to 50 ohm. The valid values are -1.2V to 1.2V if you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_LOAD_IMPEDANCE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga0ba856adbe0079fec19cc81088b5cc88.html) attribute to 100 ohm.

PXIe-5820: -0.25V to 1.5V

Note

The valid range is dependent on the load impedance.

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5645, PXIe-5820

Parent topic:

IQ Out Port

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga3183dc081843e0fb16c5cac4b9ef23cf.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00044: NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_LEVEL

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga3183dc081843e0fb16c5cac4b9ef23cf.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga3183dc081843e0fb16c5cac4b9ef23cf.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the amplitude of the generated signal in volts, peak-to-peak (V[pk-pk]). For example, if you set this attribute to 1.0, the output signal ranges from -0.5 volts to 0.5 volts. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_LEVELNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150147ViReal64Read/WriteChannelsRemarks T

### NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_LEVEL

Specifies the amplitude of the generated signal in volts, peak-to-peak (V<sub>pk-pk</sub>). For example, if you set this attribute to 1.0, the output signal ranges from -0.5 volts to 0.5 volts.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_LEVEL

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150147 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | Channels |

#### Remarks

To use this attribute, you must use the channelName parameter of the [niRFSG_SetAttributeViReal64](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1gae1e8e18281fe5567a905907fff0c7a93.html) function to specify the name of the channel you are configuring. For the PXIe-5645, you can configure the I and Q channels by using I or Q as the channel string, or set the channel string to "" (empty string) to configure both channels. For the PXIe-5820, the only valid value for the channel string is "" (empty string).

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

Note

For the PXIe-5645, this attribute is ignored if you are using the RF ports.

Refer to the specifications document for your device for allowable output levels.

**Units:** Volts, peak-to-peak (V<sub>pk-pk</sub>)

**Valid Values:**

PXIe-5645: 1 V<sub>pk-pk</sub> maximum if you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_TERMINAL_CONFIGURATION](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga9a3ee859b6e753e1ac1b2042ef1aed9b.html) attribute to **NIRFSG_VAL_DIFFERENTIAL**, and 0.5V<sub>pk-pk</sub> maximum if you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_TERMINAL_CONFIGURATION](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga9a3ee859b6e753e1ac1b2042ef1aed9b.html) attribute to **NIRFSG_VAL_SINGLE_ENDED**.

PXIe-5820: 3.4 V<sub>pk-pk</sub> maximum for signal bandwidth less than 160MHz, and 2V<sub>pk-pk</sub> maximum for signal bandwidth greater than 160MHz.

Note

The valid values are only applicable when you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_LOAD_IMPEDANCE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga0ba856adbe0079fec19cc81088b5cc88.html) attribute to 50 ohm and when you set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_OFFSET](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga21d0766f01a054e7486ea30022f4a91f.html) attribute to 0.

**Default Value:** 0.5volts

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5645, PXIe-5820

Parent topic:

IQ Out Port

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga5a69b296a7ad74aa64e3e5122b1f3b20.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00045: NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_CARRIER_FREQUENCY

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga5a69b296a7ad74aa64e3e5122b1f3b20.html`

- source_description: Specifies the frequency of the I/Q OUT port signal. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_CARRIER_FREQUENCYNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150145ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks The onboard signal processing (OSP) applies the specified frequency shift to the I/Q data before the data is sent to the digita

### NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_CARRIER_FREQUENCY

Specifies the frequency of the I/Q OUT port signal.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_CARRIER_FREQUENCY

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150145 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The onboard signal processing (OSP) applies the specified frequency shift to the I/Q data before the data is sent to the digital-to-analog converter (DAC). To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

Note

For the PXIe-5820, NI recommends using the [NIRFSG_ATTR_FREQUENCY](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga117a9c69b0efe4af03abe2c0ea4b97ae.html) attribute.

Note

For the PXIe-5645, this attribute is ignored if you are using the RF ports.

**Units:** hertz (Hz)

**Valid Values:**

PXIe-5645: -60MHz to 60MHz

PXIe-5820: -500MHz to 500MHz

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5645, PXIe-5820

## TOPIC 00047: NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_TERMINAL_CONFIGURATION

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga9a3ee859b6e753e1ac1b2042ef1aed9b.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__iq__out__port_1ga9a3ee859b6e753e1ac1b2042ef1aed9b.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to use the I/Q OUT port for differential configuration or single-ended configuration. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_TERMINAL_CONFIGURATIONNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150146ViInt32Read/WriteChannelsRemarks If you set this attribute to NIRFSG_VAL_SINGLE_ENDED, you must ter

### NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_TERMINAL_CONFIGURATION

Specifies whether to use the I/Q OUT port for differential configuration or single-ended configuration.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_IQ_OUT_PORT_TERMINAL_CONFIGURATION

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150146 | ViInt32 | Read/Write | Channels |

#### Remarks

If you set this attribute to **NIRFSG_VAL_SINGLE_ENDED**, you must terminalinate the negative I and Q output connectors with a 50 Ohm termination.

If you set this attribute to **NIRFSG_VAL_SINGLE_ENDED**, the positive I and Q connectors generate the resulting waveform. If you set this attribute to **NIRFSG_VAL_DIFFERENTIAL**, both the positive and negative I and Q connectors generate the resulting waveform.

To use this attribute, you must use the channelName parameter of the [niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt32](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1ga5ba1fecb3cc60693abe0092b4bce4e75.html) function to specify the name of the channel you are configuring. For the PXIe-5645, you can configure the I and Q channels by using I or Q as the channel string, or set the channel string to "" (empty string) to configure both channels. For the PXIe-5820, the only valid value for the channel string is "" (empty string).

Note

For the PXIe-5645, this attribute is ignored if you are using the RF ports.

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_DIFFERENTIAL | 15000 (0x3a98) | Sets the terminal configuration to differential. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_SINGLE_ENDED | 15001 (0x3a99) | Sets the terminal configuration to single-ended. |

**Default Value:****NIRFSG_VAL_DIFFERENTIAL**

PXIe-5820: The only valid value for this attribute is **NIRFSG_VAL_DIFFERENTIAL**.

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5645, PXIe-5820

**Related Topics**

[Differential and Single-Ended Operation (I/O Interface)](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/pxie-5645-feature/page/differential-single-ended-operation.html)

Parent topic:

IQ Out Port

## TOPIC 00048: NIRFSG_ATTR_LO_SOURCE

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__signal__path_1ga8dc78995221b7df54e9cd3083161d2d7.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__signal__path_1ga8dc78995221b7df54e9cd3083161d2d7.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether to use the internal or external local oscillator (LO) source. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_LO_SOURCENumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150150ViStringRead/WriteLosRemarks If the NIRFSG_ATTR_LO_SOURCE attribute is set to "" (empty string), NI-RFSG uses the internal LO source. To set this at

### NIRFSG_ATTR_LO_SOURCE

Specifies whether to use the internal or external local oscillator (LO) source.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_LO_SOURCE

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150150 | ViString | Read/Write | Los |

#### Remarks

If the [NIRFSG_ATTR_LO_SOURCE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__signal__path_1ga8dc78995221b7df54e9cd3083161d2d7.html) attribute is set to "" (empty string), NI-RFSG uses the internal LO source. To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

To use this attribute for the PXIe-5830/5831/5832, you must use the channelName parameter of the [niRFSG_SetAttributeViString](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1gacf17593f81a3f07cde9d1d6a6da635f5.html) function to specify the name of the channel you are configuring. You can configure the LO1 and LO2 channels by using lo1 or lo2 as the channel string, or set the channel string to lo1,lo2 to configure both channels. For all other devices, the the only valid value for the channel string is "" (empty string).

Note

For the PXIe-5841 with PXIe-5655, RF list mode is not supported when this attribute is set to **NIRFSG_VAL_LO_SOURCE_SG_SA_SHARED_STR**.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_LO_SOURCE_AUTOMATIC_SG_SA_SHARED_STR | Automatic_SG_SA_Shared | NI-RFSG internally makes the configuration to share the LO between NI-RFSA and NI-RFSG. This value is valid only on the PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_LO_SOURCE_LO_IN_STR | LO_In | Uses an external LO as the LO source. Connect a signal to the LO IN connector on the device and use the NIRFSG_ATTR_UPCONVERTER_CENTER_FREQUENCY attribute to specify the LO frequency. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_LO_SOURCE_ONBOARD_STR | Onboard | Uses an internal LO as the LO source. If you specify an internal LO source, the LO is generated inside the device itself. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_LO_SOURCE_SG_SA_SHARED_STR | SG_SA_Shared | Uses the same internal LO during NI-RFSA and NI-RFSG sessions. NI-RFSG selects an internal synthesizer and the synthesizer signal is switched to both the RF In and RF Out mixers. This value is valid only on the PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5841 with PXIe-5655/5842. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_LO_SOURCE_SECONDARY_STR | Secondary | Uses the PXIe-5831/5840 internal LO as the LO source. This value is valid only on the PXIe-5831 with PXIe-5653 and PXIe-5832 with PXIe-5653. |

**Default Value:****NIRFSG_VAL_LO_SOURCE_ONBOARD_STR**

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842

**Related Topics**

[PXIe-5830 LO Sharing Using NI-RFSA and NI-RFSG](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/pxie-5830-feature/page/lo-sharing-using-rfsa-rfsg.html)

[PXIe-5831/5832 LO Sharing Using NI-RFSA and NI-RFSG](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/pxie-5832-feature/page/lo-sharing-using-rfsa-rfsg.html)

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00050: NIRFSG_ATTR_ABSOLUTE_DELAY

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__signal__path_1ga9610051d13593e4064c742e487f7370b.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__signal__path_1ga9610051d13593e4064c742e487f7370b.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies the sub-Sample Clock delay, in seconds, to apply to the I/Q waveform. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ABSOLUTE_DELAYNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150225ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks Use this attribute to reduce the trigger jitter when synchronizing multiple devices with NI-TClk.This attribute ca

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ABSOLUTE_DELAY

Specifies the sub-Sample Clock delay, in seconds, to apply to the I/Q waveform.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ABSOLUTE_DELAY

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150225 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

Use this attribute to reduce the trigger jitter when synchronizing multiple devices with NI-TClk.

This attribute can also help maintain synchronization repeatability by writing the absolute delay value of a previous measurement to the current session.

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

Note

If this attribute is set, NI-TClk cannot perform any sub-Sample Clock adjustment.

Note

The resolution of this attribute is a function of the I/Q sample period at 15E(-6) times that sample period.

**Units:** Seconds

**Valid Values:** Plus or minus half of one Sample Clock period

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5820/5840/5841/5842

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00056: NIRFSG_ATTR_SYNC_START_TRIGGER_MASTER

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__triggers_1gad01f61bba72f1a8119309f6f1b64a660.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__device__specific__vector__signal__transceiver__triggers_1gad01f61bba72f1a8119309f6f1b64a660.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies whether the device is the master device when synchronizing the Start Trigger. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_SYNC_START_TRIGGER_MASTERNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150155ViBooleanRead/WriteN/ARemarks The master device distributes the synchronized Start Trigger to all devices in the system thro

### NIRFSG_ATTR_SYNC_START_TRIGGER_MASTER

Specifies whether the device is the master device when synchronizing the Start Trigger.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_SYNC_START_TRIGGER_MASTER

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150155 | ViBoolean | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The master device distributes the synchronized Start Trigger to all devices in the system through the Start Trigger distribution line.

When synchronizing the Start Trigger, one device must always be designated as the master. The master device actively drives the Start Trigger distribution line. For slave devices, set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_START_TRIGGER_TYPE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__triggers__start_1ga1bdae1da208c9b31ce9857ee4f3a1982.html) attribute to digital edge, and set the [NIRFSG_ATTR_DIGITAL_EDGE_START_TRIGGER_SOURCE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__triggers__start__digital__edge_1ga86bb4e4be0dc727203185d9270e9cbc4.html) attribute to sync_script.

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

**Defined Values:**

| Value | Description |
| --- | --- |
| VI_TRUE | The device is the master device for synchronizing the Start Trigger. |
| VI_FALSE | The device is not the master for synchronizing the Start Trigger. |

**Default Value:** VI_FALSE

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646

**Related Topics**

[Start Trigger](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/ni-rfsg-start-trigger.html)

Refer to the Synchronization Using NI-RFSA and NI-RFSG topic appropriate to your device for more information about device synchronization for vector signal transceivers.

Parent topic:

Triggers

## TOPIC 00065: NIRFSG_ATTR_ANALOG_MODULATION_AM_SENSITIVITY

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__modulation__analog_1gad9818840232448603ea85632bd9ee72b.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__modulation__analog_1gad9818840232448603ea85632bd9ee72b.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Specifies an uncalibrated digital-to-analog converter (DAC) value that scales the input signal before the signal modulates the carrier. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_ANALOG_MODULATION_AM_SENSITIVITYNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150167ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks A value of 0 completely attenuates the s

### NIRFSG_ATTR_ANALOG_MODULATION_AM_SENSITIVITY

Specifies an uncalibrated digital-to-analog converter (DAC) value that scales the input signal before the signal modulates the carrier.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ANALOG_MODULATION_AM_SENSITIVITY

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150167 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

A value of 0 completely attenuates the signal, and a value of 100 passes the full-scale signal to the modulator.

When using the PXIe-5654 with PXIe-5696, NI-RFSG may coerce AM sensitivity. Coercing the AM sensitivity prevents overpower conditions at the PXIe-5696 input. Read this attribute to determine the coerced value.

**Default Value:** 100

**Valid Values:** 0 to 100

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5654/5654 with PXIe-5696

**Related Topics**

[Amplitude Modulation](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/amplitude-modulation-am.html)

Parent topic:

Analog

## TOPIC 00068: Peer-to-Peer

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__peertopeer.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__peertopeer.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: GroupsNoneGroup membersNameDescriptionNIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_DATA_TRANSFER_PERMISSION_INITIAL_CREDITSSpecifies the initial amount of data that the writer peer can transfer over the bus into the configured endpoint when the peer-to-peer data stream is enabled. NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_DATA_TRANSFER_PERMISSION_INTERV

### Peer-to-Peer

#### Groups

None

#### Group members

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_DATA_TRANSFER_PERMISSION_INITIAL_CREDITS | Specifies the initial amount of data that the writer peer can transfer over the bus into the configured endpoint when the peer-to-peer data stream is enabled. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_DATA_TRANSFER_PERMISSION_INTERVAL | Specifies the interval at which the RF signal generator issues credits to allow the writer peer to transfer data over the bus into the configured endpoint. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_ENABLED | Specifies whether the RF signal generator reads data from the peer-to-peer endpoint. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_ENDPOINT_COUNT | Returns the number of peer-to-peer FIFO endpoints supported by the device. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_ENDPOINT_SIZE | Returns the size, in samples, of the device endpoint. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_GENERATION_FIFO_SAMPLE_QUANTUM | Returns how many samples NI-RFSG pulls from the peer-to-peer FIFO per read. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_IS_FINITE_GENERATION | Specifies whether peer-to-peer should continuously generate data from the peer-to-peer stream or from only a finite number of samples, according to the NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_NUMBER_OF_SAMPLES_TO_GENERATE attribute. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_MOST_SPACE_AVAILABLE_IN_ENDPOINT | Returns the largest number of samples per channel available in the endpoint since this attribute was last read. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_NUMBER_OF_SAMPLES_TO_GENERATE | Specifies how many samples are generated from the peer-to-peer subsystem when it is enabled. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_SPACE_AVAILABLE_IN_ENDPOINT | Returns the current space available in the endpoint. |

#### Attachments

None

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Returns how many samples NI-RFSG pulls from the peer-to-peer FIFO per read. SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_GENERATION_FIFO_SAMPLE_QUANTUMNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1150219ViInt64Read-OnlyN/ARemarks You can use this attribute to determine how many samples to send across the peer-to-peer bus to ensu

### NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_GENERATION_FIFO_SAMPLE_QUANTUM

Returns how many samples NI-RFSG pulls from the peer-to-peer FIFO per read.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_P2P_GENERATION_FIFO_SAMPLE_QUANTUM

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150219 | ViInt64 | Read-Only | N/A |

#### Remarks

You can use this attribute to determine how many samples to send across the peer-to-peer bus to ensure that no samples are ignored. If you send a number of samples that is not a multiple of this value, the remaining samples are not read from the FIFO during generation. This attribute is endpoint-based.

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842

Parent topic:

| NIRFSG_ATTR_ALLOW_OUT_OF_SPECIFICATION_USER_SETTINGS | Enables or disables warnings or errors when you set the frequency, power, and bandwidth values beyond the limits of the NI-RFSG device specifications. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_AMPLITUDE_SETTLING | Configures the amplitude settling accuracy in decibels. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ATTENUATOR_HOLD_ENABLED | Specifies whether attenuator hold is enabled. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ATTENUATOR_HOLD_MAX_POWER | Specifies the maximum power level of the RF output signal when the NIRFSG_ATTR_ATTENUATOR_HOLD_ENABLED attribute is set to VI_TRUE. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_ATTENUATOR_SETTING | Specifies the level of attenuation in the attenuator path. |

| NIRFSG_ATTR_AUTO_POWER_SEARCH | Enables or disables automatic power search. |

| NIRFSG_ATTR_FREQUENCY_TOLERANCE | Specifies the allowable frequency error introduced during the software upconversion process. |

| NIRFSG_ATTR_LO_OUT_POWER | Specifies the power level of the signal at the LO OUT front panel connector. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_OUTPUT_ENABLED | Specifies whether signal output is enabled. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_PEAK_ENVELOPE_POWER | Returns the maximum instantaneous power of the RF output signal. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_PEAK_POWER_ADJUSTMENT | Specifies the adjustment for the NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL attribute. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_PEAK_POWER_ADJUSTMENT_INHERITANCE | Determines the inheritance behavior of the NIRFSG_ATTR_PEAK_POWER_ADJUSTMENT attribute when a script inherits values from specified waveforms. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_PHASE_OFFSET | Specifies the phase of the RF output signal. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL | Specifies either the average power level or peak power level of the generated RF signal, depending on the NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL_TYPE attribute setting. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL_TYPE | Specifies how NI-RFSG interprets the value of the NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL attribute. |
| NIRFSG_ATTR_RF_IN_LO_EXPORT_ENABLED | Specifies whether to enable the RF IN LO OUT terminal on the PXIe-5840/5841. |

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`

SyntaxNIRFSG_ATTR_FREQUENCYNumeric ValueData TypeAccessApplies To1250001ViReal64Read/WriteN/ARemarks The PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672, PXIe-5820, and PXIe-5

### NIRFSG_ATTR_FREQUENCY

Specifies the frequency of the generated RF signal. For arbitrary waveform generation, this attribute specifies the center frequency of the signal.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_FREQUENCY

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1250001 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672, PXIe-5820, and PXIe-5860 must be in the Configuration state to use this attribute. However, the PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXIe-5673/5673E, and PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842 can be in the Configuration or the Generation state to use this attribute.

Note

For the PXIe-5645, this attribute is ignored if you are using the I/Q ports.

**Units**: hertz (Hz)

**Defined Values**: Refer to the specifications document for your device allowable frequency settings.

**Default Value:**

PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E: 100MHz

PXIe-5653: 4GHz

PXIe-5820: 0Hz

PXIe-5830/5831/5832: 6.5 GHz

PXIe-5840/5841/5860, PXI-5842 (500 MHz, 1 GHz, and 2 GHz bandwidth options): 1GHz

PXIe-5842 (4 GHz bandwidth option) using the Standard personality: 1GHz

PXIe-5842 (4 GHz bandwidth option) using the 4 GHz Bandwidth personality: 6.5GHz

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[NI-RFSG Instrument Driver Programming Flow](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/ni-rfsg-instrument-driver-programming-flow.html)

**High-Level Functions**:

- [niRFSG_ConfigureRF](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions_1gac15566488da784b595616805d305c82d.html)

Enables or disables warnings or errors when you set the frequency, power, and bandwidth values beyond the limits of the NI-RFSG device specifications.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_ALLOW_OUT_OF_SPECIFICATION_USER_SETTINGS

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150014 | ViInt32 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

When you enable the [NIRFSG_ATTR_ALLOW_OUT_OF_SPECIFICATION_USER_SETTINGS](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga20c95cec10a3eb35538a5b6014887863.html) attribute, the driver does not report out-of-specification warnings or errors.

To set this attribute, the NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state.

Note

Accuracy cannot be guaranteed outside of device specifications, and results may vary by module.

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_DISABLE | 0 (0x0) | Disables out-of-specification user settings. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_ENABLE | 1 (0x1) | Enables out-of-specification user settings. |

**Default Value:****NIRFSG_VAL_DISABLE**

**Supported Devices:** PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Remarks

Note

For the PXIe-5644/5645/5646 and PXIe-5673/5673E, this attribute is always read-only.

To use this attribute for the PXIe-5830/5831/5832, you must use the channelName parameter of the [niRFSG_SetAttributeViReal64](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1gae1e8e18281fe5567a905907fff0c7a93.html) function to specify the name of the channel you are configuring. You can configure the LO1 and LO2 channels by using lo1 or lo2 as the channel string, or set the channel string to lo1,lo2 to configure both channels. ### NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL

Specifies either the average power level or peak power level of the generated RF signal, depending on the [NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL_TYPE](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga57126bb84c21a6b74bc19a7f07e1ff18.html) attribute setting.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_POWER_LEVEL

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1250002 | ViReal64 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

The PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672, and PXIe-5860 must be in the Configuration state to use this attribute. However, the PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXIe-5673/5673E and PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842 can be in the Configuration or the Generation state to use this attribute.

Refer to the specifications document for your device for allowable power level settings.

Note

For the PXIe-5653, this attribute is read-only.

Note

For the PXIe-5645, this attribute is ignored if you are using the I/Q ports.

**Units**: dBm

**Default Values:**

PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5673/5673E: -100

PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652: -90

PXIe-5654: -7

PXIe-5654 with PXIe-5696: -110

PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672: -145

PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860: -174

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860 **High-Level Functions**:

- [niRFSG_ConfigureRF](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions_1gac15566488da784b595616805d305c82d.html)

Parent topic:

RF

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

### NIRFSG_ATTR_PEAK_POWER_ADJUSTMENT_INHERITANCE

Determines the inheritance behavior of the [NIRFSG_ATTR_PEAK_POWER_ADJUSTMENT](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1ga17dddd332f64d3d4dc9a4359a96894f4.html) attribute when a script inherits values from specified waveforms.

#### Syntax

NIRFSG_ATTR_PEAK_POWER_ADJUSTMENT_INHERITANCE

| Numeric Value | Data Type | Access | Applies To |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1150141 | ViInt32 | Read/Write | N/A |

#### Remarks

**Defined Values:**

| Name | Value | Description |
| --- | --- | --- |
| NIRFSG_VAL_EXACT_MATCH | 0 (0x0) | Errors out if different values are detected in the script. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_MAXIMUM | 2 (0x2) | Uses the maximum value found in the script. |
| NIRFSG_VAL_MINIMUM | 1 (0x1) | Uses the minimum value found in the script. |

**Default Value:****NIRFSG_VAL_EXACT_MATCH**

**Supported Devices:** PXIe-5673/5673E
