## TOPIC 00136: niRFSG_WriteScript

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__scripting_1gac5d4483a4ad7dc2714037a6efbf09f84.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__scripting_1gac5d4483a4ad7dc2714037a6efbf09f84.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Writes a script to the device to control waveform generation in Script mode. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_WriteScript(ViSession vi, ViConstString script)RemarksFirst, configure your device for Script mode by calling the niRFSG_ConfigureGenerationMode function. The NI-RFSG device must be in the Co

### niRFSG_WriteScript

Writes a script to the device to control waveform generation in Script mode.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_WriteScript(ViSession vi, ViConstString script)

#### Remarks

First, configure your device for Script mode by calling the [niRFSG_ConfigureGenerationMode](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__configure__waveform_1ga7b0515c71bce7bebe6c57204cb5539bf.html) function. The NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state before calling the [niRFSG_WriteScript](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__scripting_1gac5d4483a4ad7dc2714037a6efbf09f84.html) function.

Note

If you are using an RF vector signal transceiver (VST) device, some script instructions may not be supported.

**Supported Devices**: PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Scripting Instructions](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/scripting-instructions.html)–Refer to this topic for more information about VST restrictions on scripts.

[Common Scripting Use Cases](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/common-scripting-use-cases.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| script | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies a string containing a syntactically correct script. NI-RFSG supports multiple scripts that are selected with the NIRFSG_ATTR_SELECTED_SCRIPT attribute. Refer to Scripting Instructions for more information about using scripts. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

### niRFSG_GetScript

Returns the content of specified script.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_GetScript(ViSession vi, ViConstString scriptName, ViChar script[], ViInt32 bufferSize, ViInt32 *actualBufferSize)

#### Remarks

**Supported Devices**: PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| scriptName | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies the name of the script to retrieve. This string is case-insensitive. |
| script | [out] | ViChar[] | Returns the script. |
| bufferSize | [in] | ViInt32 | Pass the number of bytes in the ViChar buffer you specify for the script parameter.If you pass 0, you can pass VI_NULL for the script parameter. |
| actualBufferSize | [out] | ViInt32 * | Fetch the number of bytes needed to pass in the bufferSize parameter.It can be fetched by passing VI_NULL in the script parameter. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. | Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

### niRFSG_CheckAttributeViSession

Checks the validity of a value you specify for a ViSession attribute.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_CheckAttributeViSession(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViSession value)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| channelName | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies the waveform name and the marker name.Example:"waveform::waveform0/marker0" |
| attribute | [in] | ViAttr | Pass the ID of an attribute. |
| value | [in] | ViSession | Pass the value that you want to verify as a valid value for the attribute.Note Some of the values might not be valid depending on the current settings of the instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

## TOPIC 00144: niRFSG_GetAttributeViInt64

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_GetAttributeViInt64(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt64 *value)RemarksYou can use this low-level function to get the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and instrument-sp

### niRFSG_GetAttributeViInt64

Queries the value of a ViInt64 attribute.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_GetAttributeViInt64(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt64 *value)

#### Remarks

You can use this low-level function to get the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and instrument-specific attributes. If the attribute represents an instrument state, this function performs instrument I/O in the following cases:

- State caching is disabled for the entire session or for the particular attribute.
- State caching is enabled, and the currently cached value is invalid.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| channelName | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies the waveform name and the marker name.Example:"waveform::waveform0/marker0" |
| attribute | [in] | ViAttr | Pass the ID of an attribute. |
| value | [out] | ViInt64 * | Returns the current value of the attribute. Pass the address of a ViInt64 variable. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

## TOPIC 00149: niRFSG_GetAttributeViString

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__get__attribute_1gae28cf726cd54643eabee88cb0f01a988.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__get__attribute_1gae28cf726cd54643eabee88cb0f01a988.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Queries the value of a ViString attribute. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_GetAttributeViString(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt32 bufSize, ViChar value[])RemarksUse this low-level function to get the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and in

### niRFSG_GetAttributeViString

Queries the value of a ViString attribute.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_GetAttributeViString(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt32 bufSize, ViChar value[])

#### Remarks

Use this low-level function to get the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and instrument-specific attributes. If the attribute represents an instrument state, this function performs instrument I/O in the following cases:

- State caching is disabled for the entire session or for the particular attribute.
- State caching is enabled, and the currently cached value is invalid.

You must provide a ViString (ViChar array) to serve as a buffer for the value. Pass the number of bytes in the buffer as the Buffer Size parameter. If the current value of the attribute, including the terminating NULL byte, is larger than the size you indicate in the buffer size parameter, the function copies buffer size-1 bytes into the buffer, places an ASCII NULL byte at the end of the buffer, and returns the buffer size you must pass to get the entire value. For example, if the value is "123456" and the buffer size is 4, the function places "123" into the buffer and returns 7.

To call this function to get only the required buffer size, pass 0 for the buffer size and VI_NULL for the attribute value buffer.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| channelName | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies the waveform name and the marker name.Example:"waveform::waveform0/marker0" |
| attribute | [in] | ViAttr | Pass the ID of an attribute. |
| bufSize | [in] | ViInt32 | Pass the number of bytes in the ViChar buffer you specify for the waveformNames parameter.If you pass 0, you can pass VI_NULL for the waveformNames parameter. |
| value | [out] | ViChar[] | The buffer in which the function returns the current value of the attribute. The buffer must be of type ViChar and have at least as many bytes as indicated in the bufferSize parameter.If you specify 0 for the bufferSize parameter, you can pass VI_NULL for this parameter. |

#### Returns

gets the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Get Attribute

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute.html language=enus -->

## TOPIC 00151: niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt64

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1ga165aff0da447ad3c8e528039c2f255d2.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1ga165aff0da447ad3c8e528039c2f255d2.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Sets the value of a ViInt64 attribute. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt64(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt64 value)RemarksUse this low-level function to set the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and instrument-specific attri

### niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt64

Sets the value of a ViInt64 attribute.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt64(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt64 value)

#### Remarks

Use this low-level function to set the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and instrument-specific attributes. If the attribute represents an instrument state, this function performs instrument I/O in the following cases:

- State caching is disabled for the entire session or for the particular attribute.
- State caching is enabled, and the currently cached value is invalid or is different than the value you specify.

NI-RFSG contains high-level functions that set most of the instrument attributes. Use the high-level driver functions as much as possible, as they handle order dependencies and multithread locking. The high-level functions also perform status checking only after setting all of the attributes. In contrast, when you set multiple attributes using the SetAttribute functions, the functions check the instrument status after each call.

Also, when state caching is enabled, the high-level functions that configure multiple attributes perform instrument I/O only for the attributes whose value you change. Thus, you can safely call the high-level functions without the penalty of redundant instrument I/O.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| channelName | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies the waveform name and the marker name.Example:"waveform::waveform0/marker0" |
| attribute | [in] | ViAttr | Pass the ID of an attribute. |
| value | [in] | ViInt64 | Pass the value to which you want to set the attribute.Note Some values may not be valid. The allowed values depend on the current settings of the instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

## TOPIC 00152: niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt32

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1ga5ba1fecb3cc60693abe0092b4bce4e75.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__generation__configuration__setgetcheck__attribute__set__attribute_1ga5ba1fecb3cc60693abe0092b4bce4e75.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Sets the value of a ViInt32 attribute. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt32(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt32 value)RemarksUse this low-level function to set the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and instrument-specific attri

### niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt32

Sets the value of a ViInt32 attribute.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_SetAttributeViInt32(ViSession vi, ViConstString channelName, ViAttr attribute, ViInt32 value)

#### Remarks

Use this low-level function to set the values of inherent IVI attributes, class-defined attributes, and instrument-specific attributes. If the attribute represents an instrument state, this function performs instrument I/O in the following cases:

- State caching is disabled for the entire session or for the particular attribute.
- State caching is enabled, and the currently cached value is invalid or is different than the value you specify.

NI-RFSG contains high-level functions that set most of the instrument attributes. Use the high-level driver functions as much as possible, as they handle order dependencies and multithread locking. The high-level functions also perform status checking only after setting all of the attributes. In contrast, when you set multiple attributes using the SetAttribute functions, the functions check the instrument status after each call.

Also, when state caching is enabled, the high-level functions that configure multiple attributes perform instrument I/O only for the attributes whose value you change. Thus, you can safely call the high-level functions without the penalty of redundant instrument I/O.

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| channelName | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies the waveform name and the marker name.Example:"waveform::waveform0/marker0" |
| attribute | [in] | ViAttr | Pass the ID of an attribute. |
| value | [in] | ViInt32 | Specifies the value to which you want to set the attribute.Note Some values may not be valid. The allowed values depend on the current settings of the instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

## TOPIC 00157: Utility

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: GroupsError InfoLockingGroup membersNameDescriptionniRFSG_CommitPrograms the device with the correct settings. niRFSG_DisablePlaces the instrument in a quiescent state where it has minimal or no impact on the system to which it is connected. niRFSG_GetChannelNameReturns the channel string that is in

### Utility

#### Groups

- Error Info
- Locking

#### Group members

| Name | Description |
| --- | --- |
| niRFSG_Commit | Programs the device with the correct settings. |
| niRFSG_Disable | Places the instrument in a quiescent state where it has minimal or no impact on the system to which it is connected. |
| niRFSG_GetChannelName | Returns the channel string that is in the channel table at an index you specify. |
| niRFSG_GetMaxSettablePower | Returns the maximum settable output power level for the current configuration. |
| niRFSG_InitWithOptions | Opens a session to the device you specify as the resourceName and returns a ViSession handle that you use to identify the NI-RFSG device in all subsequent NI-RFSG function calls. |
| niRFSG_LoadConfigurationsFromFile | Loads the configurations from the specified file to the NI-RFSG driver session. |
| niRFSG_PerformPowerSearch | Performs a power search if the NIRFSG_ATTR_ALC_CONTROL attribute is disabled. |
| niRFSG_PerformThermalCorrection | Corrects for any signal drift due to environmental temperature variation when generating the same signal for extended periods of time without a parameter change. |
| niRFSG_QueryArbWaveformCapabilities | Queries and returns the waveform capabilities of the NI-RFSG device. |
| niRFSG_Reset | Resets all attributes to their default values and moves the NI-RFSG device to the Configuration state. |
| niRFSG_ResetDevice | Performs a hard reset on the device which consists of the following actions: |
| niRFSG_ResetWithDefaults | Performs a software reset of the device, returning it to the default state and applying any initial default settings from the IVI Configuration Store. |
| niRFSG_ResetWithOptions | Resets all properties to default values and specifies steps to omit during the reset process, such as signal routes. |
| niRFSG_RevisionQuery | Returns the revision numbers of the NI-RFSG driver and the instrument firmware. |
| niRFSG_SaveConfigurationsToFile | Saves the configurations of the session to the specified file. |
| niRFSG_SelfTest | Performs a self-test on the NI-RFSG device and returns the test results. |
| niRFSG_WaitUntilSettled | Waits until the RF output signal has settled. This function is useful for devices that support changes while in the Generation state. |

#### Attachments

None

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga017a2dd798bbd528ee06c44e2e69a504.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00158: niRFSG_InitWithOptions

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga017a2dd798bbd528ee06c44e2e69a504.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga017a2dd798bbd528ee06c44e2e69a504.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Opens a session to the device you specify as the resourceName and returns a ViSession handle that you use to identify the NI-RFSG device in all subsequent NI-RFSG function calls. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_InitWithOptions(ViRsrc resourceName, ViBoolean idQuery, ViBoolean resetDevice, ViConstStr

### niRFSG_InitWithOptions

Opens a session to the device you specify as the **resourceName** and returns a ViSession handle that you use to identify the NI-RFSG device in all subsequent NI-RFSG function calls.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_InitWithOptions(ViRsrc resourceName, ViBoolean idQuery, ViBoolean resetDevice, ViConstString optionString, ViSession *newVi)

#### Remarks

This function also configures the device through the **optionString** input.

Note

For multichannel devices such as the PXIe-5860, the resource name must include the channel number to use. The channel number is specified by appending /*ChannelNumber* to the device name, where *ChannelNumber* is the channel number (0, 1, etc.). For example, if the device name is PXI1Slot2 and you want to use channel 0, use the resource name PXI1Slot2/0.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Simulating an NI RF Signal Generator](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/simulating-a-device.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| resourceName | [in] | ViRsrc | Specifies the resource name of the device to initialize.For NI-DAQmx devices, the syntax is the device name specified in MAX. Typical default names for NI-DAQmx devices in MAX are Dev2 or PXISlot2. You can rename an NI-DAQmx device in MAX.You can also specify the name of an IVI logical name configured with the IVI Configuration utility. Refer to the IVI topic of the Measurement & Automation Explorer Help for more information.Note NI-RFSG device names are not case-sensitive. However, all IVI names, such as logical names, are case-sensitive. If you use an IVI logical name, make sure the name is identical to the name shown in the IVI Configuration Utility. |
| idQuery | [in] | ViBoolean | Specifies whether you want NI-RFSG to perform an ID query.Defined Values:ValueDescriptionVI_TRUE (1)Perform ID query.VI_FALSE (0)Do not perform ID query. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| VI_TRUE (1) | Perform ID query. |  |  |
| VI_FALSE (0) | Do not perform ID query. |  |  |
| resetDevice | [in] | ViBoolean | Specifies whether you want to reset the NI-RFSG device during the initialization procedure.Defined Values:ValueDescriptionVI_TRUE (1)Reset device.VI_FALSE (0)Do not reset device. |
| Value | Description |  |  |
| VI_TRUE (1) | Reset device. |  |  |
| VI_FALSE (0) | Do not reset device. |  |  |
| optionString | [in] | ViConstString | Specifies the initial value of certain attributes for the session. The following table lists the attributes and the name you pass in this parameter to identify the attribute.NameAttribute NameRangeCheckNIRFSG_ATTR_RANGE_CHECKQueryInstrStatusNIRFSG_ATTR_QUERY_INSTRUMENT_STATUSCacheNIRFSG_ATTR_CACHERecordCoercionsNIRFSG_ATTR_RECORD_COERCIONSSimulateNIRFSG_ATTR_SIMULATEThe format of this string consists of the following relations: "AttributeName=Value"where AttributeName is the name of the attribute and Value is the value to which the attribute is set. To set multiple attributes, separate their assignments with a comma, as shown in the following option string:"RangeCheck=1,QueryInstrStatus=0,Cache=1,DriverSetup=AWG:pxi1slot4"The DriverSetup string is required in order to simulate a specific device. |
| Name | Attribute Name |  |  |
| RangeCheck | NIRFSG_ATTR_RANGE_CHECK |  |  |
| QueryInstrStatus | NIRFSG_ATTR_QUERY_INSTRUMENT_STATUS |  |  |
| Cache | NIRFSG_ATTR_CACHE |  |  |
| RecordCoercions | NIRFSG_ATTR_RECORD_COERCIONS |  |  |
| Simulate | NIRFSG_ATTR_SIMULATE |  |  |
| newVi | [out] | ViSession * | Returns a ViSession handle that you use to identify the NI-RFSG device in all subsequent NI-RFSG function calls. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. ## TOPIC 00161: niRFSG_ResetDevice

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga3cc2607cfc2ab4c6d358dc1ef8ee2d83.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga3cc2607cfc2ab4c6d358dc1ef8ee2d83.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Performs a hard reset on the device which consists of the following actions: SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_ResetDevice(ViSession vi)RemarksSignal generation is stopped.All routes are released.External bidirectional terminals are tristated.FPGAs are reset.Hardware is configured to its default state

### niRFSG_ResetDevice

Performs a hard reset on the device which consists of the following actions:

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_ResetDevice(ViSession vi)

#### Remarks

- Signal generation is stopped.
- All routes are released.
- External bidirectional terminals are tristated.
- FPGAs are reset.
- Hardware is configured to its default state.
- All session attributes are reset to their default states.

During a device reset, routes of signals between this and other devices are released, regardless of which device created the route.

- PXI-5610, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672– After calling this function, the device requires 25 seconds before returning to full functionality. NI-RFSG enforces this condition by adding a wait, if needed, the next time you try to access the device.

Note

You must call the [niRFSG_ResetDevice](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga3cc2607cfc2ab4c6d358dc1ef8ee2d83.html) function if the NI-RFSG device has shut down because of a high-temperature condition.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E

**Related Topics**

[Thermal Shutdown](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/thermal-shutdown.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Utility

## TOPIC 00162: niRFSG_Reset

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga68e388e0f332b908aa71cc03dcc74583.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga68e388e0f332b908aa71cc03dcc74583.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Resets all attributes to their default values and moves the NI-RFSG device to the Configuration state. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_Reset(ViSession vi)RemarksThis function aborts the generation, deletes all de-embedding tables, clears all routes, and resets session attributes to their initial val

### niRFSG_Reset

Resets all attributes to their default values and moves the NI-RFSG device to the Configuration state.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_Reset(ViSession vi)

#### Remarks

This function aborts the generation, deletes all de-embedding tables, clears all routes, and resets session attributes to their initial values. During a reset, routes of signals between this and other devices are released, regardless of which device created the route.

Generally, calling this function instead of the [niRFSG_ResetDevice](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga3cc2607cfc2ab4c6d358dc1ef8ee2d83.html) function is acceptable. The [niRFSG_Reset](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga68e388e0f332b908aa71cc03dcc74583.html) function executes faster than the [niRFSG_ResetDevice](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga3cc2607cfc2ab4c6d358dc1ef8ee2d83.html) function.

To avoid resetting routes on the PXIe-5644/5645/5646 and PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860 that are in use by NI-RFSA sessions, NI recommends using the [niRFSG_ResetWithOptions](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga86c87a8758c8fc1f2f9c9be2aaf3fc03.html) function, with **stepsToOmit** set to **NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_ROUTES** .

Note

This function resets all configured routes for the PXIe-5644/5645/5646 and PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860 in NI-RFSA and NI-RFSG.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Utility

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga6bcccd63dbf666d5962a30c87555cbe3.html language=enus -->

## TOPIC 00164: niRFSG_PerformThermalCorrection

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga81c9e40c16289322bc873dfc2d08e724.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga81c9e40c16289322bc873dfc2d08e724.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Corrects for any signal drift due to environmental temperature variation when generating the same signal for extended periods of time without a parameter change. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_PerformThermalCorrection(ViSession vi)RemarksUnder normal circumstances of short-term signal generation, N

### niRFSG_PerformThermalCorrection

Corrects for any signal drift due to environmental temperature variation when generating the same signal for extended periods of time without a parameter change.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_PerformThermalCorrection(ViSession vi)

#### Remarks

Under normal circumstances of short-term signal generation, NI-RFSG performs thermal correction automatically by ensuring stable power levels, and you do not need to call this function.

Use this function when generating the same signal for an extended period of time in a temperature-fluctuating environment. The NI-RFSG device must be in the Generation state before calling this function.

**Supported Devices**: PXIe-5611, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Thermal Management](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/thermal-management.html)

[Impairment Calibration](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/impairment-calibration.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. | Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |

| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

## TOPIC 00165: niRFSG_ResetWithOptions

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga86c87a8758c8fc1f2f9c9be2aaf3fc03.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga86c87a8758c8fc1f2f9c9be2aaf3fc03.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Resets all properties to default values and specifies steps to omit during the reset process, such as signal routes. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_ResetWithOptions(ViSession vi, ViUInt64 stepsToOmit)RemarksBy default, this function exhibits the same behavior as niRFSG_Reset. You can specify steps

### niRFSG_ResetWithOptions

Resets all properties to default values and specifies steps to omit during the reset process, such as signal routes.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_ResetWithOptions(ViSession vi, ViUInt64 stepsToOmit)

#### Remarks

By default, this function exhibits the same behavior as [niRFSG_Reset](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga68e388e0f332b908aa71cc03dcc74583.html). You can specify steps to omit using the steps to omit parameter. For example, if you specify **NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_ROUTES** for the **stepsToOmit** parameter, this function does not release signal routes during the reset process.

When routes of signals between two devices are released, they are released regardless of which device created the route.

To avoid resetting routes on PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860 that are in use by NI-RFSA sessions, NI recommends using this function instead of [niRFSG_Reset](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga68e388e0f332b908aa71cc03dcc74583.html), with **stepsToOmit** set to **NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_ROUTES**.

**Supported Devices**: PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Triggers](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/ni-rfsg-triggers.html)

[Events](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/ni-rfsg-supported-events.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| stepsToOmit | [in] | ViUInt64 | Specifies a list of steps to skip during the reset process. The default value is NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_NONE, which specifies that no step is omitted during reset.Defined Values:NameValueDescriptionNIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_DEEMBEDDING_TABLES8 (0x8)Omits deleting de-embedding tables. This step is valid only for the PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840.NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_NONE0 (0x0)No step is omitted during reset.NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_ROUTES4 (0x4)Omits the routing reset step. Routing is preserved after a reset. However, routing related properties are reset to default, and routing is released if the default properties are committed after a reset.NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_SCRIPTS2 (0x2)Omits clearing scripts.NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_WAVEFORMS1 (0x1)Omits clearing waveforms.Note NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_ROUTES is not supported in external calibration or alignment sessions. |
| Name | Value | Description |  |
| NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_DEEMBEDDING_TABLES | 8 (0x8) | Omits deleting de-embedding tables. This step is valid only for the PXIe-5830/5831/5832/5840. |  |
| NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_NONE | 0 (0x0) | No step is omitted during reset. |  |
| NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_ROUTES | 4 (0x4) | Omits the routing reset step. Routing is preserved after a reset. However, routing related properties are reset to default, and routing is released if the default properties are committed after a reset. |  |
| NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_SCRIPTS | 2 (0x2) | Omits clearing scripts. |  |
| NIRFSG_VAL_RESET_WITH_OPTIONS_WAVEFORMS | 1 (0x1) | Omits clearing waveforms. |  |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Utility

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga91ce6322f28a06fd430d074967013b0e.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00166: niRFSG_Commit

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga91ce6322f28a06fd430d074967013b0e.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga91ce6322f28a06fd430d074967013b0e.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Programs the device with the correct settings. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_Commit(ViSession vi)RemarksCalling this function moves the NI-RFSG device from the Configuration state to the Committed state. After this function executes, a change to any attribute reverts the NI-RFSG device to the Conf

### niRFSG_Commit

Programs the device with the correct settings.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_Commit(ViSession vi)

#### Remarks

Calling this function moves the NI-RFSG device from the Configuration state to the Committed state. After this function executes, a change to any attribute reverts the NI-RFSG device to the Configuration state.

**Supported devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[NI-RFSG Programming State Model](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/ni-rfsg-programming-state-model.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |

#### Returns

## TOPIC 00167: niRFSG_SelfTest

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gaad2e8c35e3ecb845b2e41577f6678b95.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gaad2e8c35e3ecb845b2e41577f6678b95.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Performs a self-test on the NI-RFSG device and returns the test results. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_SelfTest(ViSession vi, ViInt16 *selfTestResult, ViChar selfTestMessage[IVI_MAX_MESSAGE_BUF_SIZE])RemarksThis function performs a simple series of tests to ensure that the NI-RFSG device is powere

### niRFSG_SelfTest

Performs a self-test on the NI-RFSG device and returns the test results.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_SelfTest(ViSession vi, ViInt16 *selfTestResult, ViChar selfTestMessage[IVI_MAX_MESSAGE_BUF_SIZE])

#### Remarks

This function performs a simple series of tests to ensure that the NI-RFSG device is powered up and responding.

This function does not affect external I/O connections or connections between devices. Complete functional testing and calibration are not performed by this function. The NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration state before you call this function.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

**Related Topics**

[Device Warm-Up](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/device-warm-up.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| selfTestResult | [out] | ViInt16 * | This parameter contains the value returned from the NI-RFSG device self test.Self-Test CodeDescription0Self test passed1Self test failed |
| Self-Test Code | Description |  |  |
| 0 | Self test passed |  |  |
| 1 | Self test failed |  |  |
| selfTestMessage | [in] | ViChar[IVI_MAX_MESSAGE_BUF_SIZE] | Returns the self-test response string from the NI-RFSG device. For an explanation of the string contents, refer to the status parameter of this function.You must pass a ViChar array with at least 256 bytes. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Utility

## TOPIC 00171: niRFSG_WaitUntilSettled

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gacb08f708c64c5f1f700dd1da0321d1ef.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gacb08f708c64c5f1f700dd1da0321d1ef.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Waits until the RF output signal has settled. This function is useful for devices that support changes while in the Generation state. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_WaitUntilSettled(ViSession vi, ViInt32 maxTimeMilliseconds)RemarksCall this function after making a dynamic change to wait for the out

### niRFSG_WaitUntilSettled

Waits until the RF output signal has settled. This function is useful for devices that support changes while in the Generation state.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_WaitUntilSettled(ViSession vi, ViInt32 maxTimeMilliseconds)

#### Remarks

Call this function after making a dynamic change to wait for the output signal to settle.

You can also call this function after calling the [niRFSG_Commit](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga91ce6322f28a06fd430d074967013b0e.html) function to wait for changes to settle. The [niRFSG_WaitUntilSettled](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gacb08f708c64c5f1f700dd1da0321d1ef.html) function is not required after calling the [niRFSG_Initiate](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions_1ga31ed10584ebd85f37876b131d6a36335.html) function because the [niRFSG_Initiate](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions_1ga31ed10584ebd85f37876b131d6a36335.html) automatically waits for the output to settle.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| maxTimeMilliseconds | [in] | ViInt32 | Specifies the maximum time the function waits for the output to settle. If the maximum time is exceeded, this function returns an error. The units are expressed in milliseconds.Default Value: 10000 |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Utility

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gacd105a094729b1ac2a622705777e4353.html language=enus -->

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`

- content_type: `reference`

SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_QueryArbWaveformCapabilities(ViSession vi, ViInt32 *maxNumberWaveforms, ViInt32 *waveformQuantum, ViInt32 *minWaveformSize, ViInt32 *maxWaveformSize)RemarksThese capabilities are related to the curre

### niRFSG_QueryArbWaveformCapabilities

Queries and returns the waveform capabilities of the NI-RFSG device.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_QueryArbWaveformCapabilities(ViSession vi, ViInt32 *maxNumberWaveforms, ViInt32 *waveformQuantum, ViInt32 *minWaveformSize, ViInt32 *maxWaveformSize)

#### Remarks

These capabilities are related to the current device configuration. The NI-RFSG device must be in the Configuration or the Generation state before calling this function.

**Supported Devices**: PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5830/5831/5832/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| maxNumberWaveforms | [out] | ViInt32 * | Returns the value of the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_MAX_NUMBER_WAVEFORMS attribute. This value is the maximum number of waveforms you can write. |
| waveformQuantum | [out] | ViInt32 * | Returns the value of the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_QUANTUM attribute. If the waveform quantum is q, then the size of the waveform that you write should be a multiple of q. The units are expressed in samples. |
| minWaveformSize | [out] | ViInt32 * | Returns the value of the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_SIZE_MIN attribute. The number of samples of the waveform that you write must be greater than or equal to this value. |
| maxWaveformSize | [out] | ViInt32 * | Returns the value of the NIRFSG_ATTR_ARB_WAVEFORM_SIZE_MAX attribute. The number of samples of the waveform that you write must be less than or equal to this value. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

## TOPIC 00173: niRFSG_PerformPowerSearch

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gade154341765bc6c447a7f85ac03c9878.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1gade154341765bc6c447a7f85ac03c9878.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Performs a power search if the NIRFSG_ATTR_ALC_CONTROL attribute is disabled. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_PerformPowerSearch(ViSession vi)RemarksCalling this function disables modulation for a short time while the device levels the output signal.Power search temporarily enables the ALC, so ensur

### niRFSG_PerformPowerSearch

Performs a power search if the [NIRFSG_ATTR_ALC_CONTROL](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__attributes__rf_1gadd660f04c6b19a63e7fbd36da14be6ac.html) attribute is disabled.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_PerformPowerSearch(ViSession vi)

#### Remarks

Calling this function disables modulation for a short time while the device levels the output signal.

Note

Power search temporarily enables the ALC, so ensure the appropriate included cable is connected between the PXIe-5654 ALCIN connector and the PXIe-5696 ALCOUT connector to successfully perform a power search.

**Supported Devices**: PXIe-5654 with PXIe-5696

**Related Topics**

[Power Search](https://www.ni.com/docs/en-US/bundle/ni-rfsg/page/5654-power-search.html)

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

| niRFSG_ClearError | Clears the error information associated with the session. |
| niRFSG_ErrorMessage | Converts an error code returned by an NI-RFSG function into a user-readable string. |
| niRFSG_ErrorQuery | Reads an error code and an error message from the instrument error queue. |
| niRFSG_GetError | Retrieves and then clears the IVI error information for the session or the current execution thread. |

#### Attachments

None

## TOPIC 00176: niRFSG_ClearError

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga3688d1b3ca7c7d05b74cb79149a279df.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga3688d1b3ca7c7d05b74cb79149a279df.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Clears the error information associated with the session. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_ClearError(ViSession vi)RemarksIf you pass VI_NULL for the vi parameter, this function clears the error information for the current execution thread.The niRFSG_GetError function clears the error information aft

### niRFSG_ClearError

Clears the error information associated with the session.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_ClearError(ViSession vi)

#### Remarks

If you pass VI_NULL for the **vi** parameter, this function clears the error information for the current execution thread.

Note

The [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function clears the error information after it is retrieved. A call to the [niRFSG_ClearError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga3688d1b3ca7c7d05b74cb79149a279df.html) function is necessary only when you do not use a call to the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function to retrieve error information.

The IVI Engine also maintains this error information separately for each thread. This feature of the IVI Engine is useful if you do not have a session handle to pass to the [niRFSG_ClearError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga3688d1b3ca7c7d05b74cb79149a279df.html) function or the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function, which occurs when a call to the [niRFSG_Init](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions_1gaf8c22002a017023ec41899d8d7762ac6.html) function or the [niRFSG_InitWithOptions](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility_1ga017a2dd798bbd528ee06c44e2e69a504.html) function fails.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

## TOPIC 00178: niRFSG_GetError

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Retrieves and then clears the IVI error information for the session or the current execution thread. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_GetError(ViSession vi, ViStatus *errorCode, ViInt32 errorDescriptionBufferSize, ViChar errorDescription[])RemarksIf the bufferSize parameter is 0, this function does n

### niRFSG_GetError

Retrieves and then clears the IVI error information for the session or the current execution thread.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_GetError(ViSession vi, ViStatus *errorCode, ViInt32 errorDescriptionBufferSize, ViChar errorDescription[])

#### Remarks

Note

If the **bufferSize** parameter is 0, this function does not clear the error information. By passing 0 to the **bufferSize** parameter, you can determine the buffer size required to obtain the entire **errorDescription** string. You can then call this function again with a sufficiently large buffer. If you specify a valid IVI session for the **vi** parameter, this function retrieves and clears the error information for the session. If you pass VI_NULL for the **vi** parameter, this function retrieves and clears the error information for the current execution thread. If the **vi** parameter is an invalid session, this function does nothing and returns an error. Normally, the error information describes the first error that occurred since the user last called this function or the [niRFSG_ClearError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga3688d1b3ca7c7d05b74cb79149a279df.html) function.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5653/5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| errorCode | [out] | ViStatus * | Returns the error code for the session or execution thread. If you pass 0 for the BufferSize parameter, you can pass VI_NULL for this parameter. |
| errorDescriptionBufferSize | [in] | ViInt32 | Pass the number of bytes in the ViChar array you specify for the description parameter.If the errorDescription, including the terminating NULL byte, contains more bytes than you indicate in this parameter, the function copies bufferSize - 1 bytes into the buffer, places an ASCII NULL byte at the end of the buffer, and returns the buffer size you must pass to get the entire value. Forexample, if the value is 123456 and the buffer size is 4, the function places 123 into the buffer and returns 7. If you pass 0, you can pass VI_NULL for the description parameter.Default Value: None |
| errorDescription | [out] | ViChar[] | Returns the errorDescription for the IVI session or execution thread.If there is no description, the function returns an empty string. The buffer must contain at least as many elements as the value you specify with the bufferSize parameter. If the errorDescription, including the terminating NULL byte, contains more bytes than you indicate with the bufferSize parameter, the function copies bufferSize - 1 bytes into the buffer, places an ASCII NULL byte at the end of the buffer, and returns the buffer size you must pass to get the entire value. For example, if the value is 123456 and the buffer size is 4, the function places 123 into the buffer and returns 7. If you pass 0, you can pass VI_NULL for this parameter. |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Error Info

## TOPIC 00181: niRFSG_LockSession

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Obtains a multithread lock on the instrument session. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_LockSession(ViSession vi, ViBoolean *callerHasLock)RemarksBefore doing so, this function waits until all other execution threads have released their locks on the instrument session.Other threads might have obtained

### niRFSG_LockSession

Obtains a multithread lock on the instrument session.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_LockSession(ViSession vi, ViBoolean *callerHasLock)

#### Remarks

Before doing so, this function waits until all other execution threads have released their locks on the instrument session.

Other threads might have obtained a lock on this session in the following ways:

- Your application already called the [niRFSG_LockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html) function.
- A call to NI-RFSG locked the session.

After the call to this function returns successfully, no other threads can access the instrument session until you call the [niRFSG_UnlockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html) function. Use the [niRFSG_LockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html) function and the [niRFSG_UnlockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html) function around a sequence of calls to NI-RFSG functions if you require that the NI-RFSG device retain its settings through the end of the sequence.

You can safely make nested calls to the [niRFSG_LockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html) function within the same thread. To completely unlock the session, balance each call to the [niRFSG_LockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html) function with a call to the [niRFSG_UnlockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html) function. If, however, you use the **callerHasLock** parameter in all calls to the [niRFSG_LockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html) function and the [niRFSG_UnlockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html) function within a function, the IVI Library locks the session only once within the function regardless of the number of calls you make to the [niRFSG_LockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html) function. Locking the session only once allows you to call [niRFSG_UnlockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html) just once at the end of the function.

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| callerHasLock | [out] | ViBoolean * | Keeps track of whether you obtain a lock and therefore need to unlock the session. Pass the address of a local ViBoolean variable. In the declaration of the local variable, initialize it to VI_FALSE. Pass the address of the same local variable to any other calls you make to the niRFSG_LockSession function or the niRFSG_UnlockSession function in the same function.This parameter serves as a convenience. If you do not want to use this parameter, pass VI_NULL.The parameter is an input/output parameter. The niRFSG_LockSession function and the niRFSG_UnlockSession each inspect the current value and take the following actions:If the value is VI_TRUE, the niRFSG_LockSession function does not lock the session again. If the value is VI_FALSE, the niRFSG_LockSession function obtains the lock and sets the value of the parameter to VI_TRUE.If the value is VI_FALSE, the niRFSG_UnlockSession function does not attempt to unlock the session. If the value is VI_TRUE, the niRFSG_UnlockSession function releases the lock and sets the value of the parameter to VI_FALSE.Thus, you can call the niRFSG_UnlockSession function at the end of your function without worrying about whether you have the lock.Example:ViStatus TestFunc (ViSession vi, ViInt32 flags) { ViStatus error = VI_SUCCESS; ViBoolean haveLock = VI_FALSE;if (flags & BIT_1) { viCheckErr( niRFSG_LockSession(vi, &haveLock)); viCheckErr( TakeAction1(vi)); if (flags & BIT_2) { viCheckErr( niRFSG_UnlockSession(vi, &haveLock)); viCheckErr( TakeAction2(vi)); viCheckErr( niRFSG_LockSession(vi, &haveLock)); } if (flags & BIT_3) viCheckErr( TakeAction3(vi)); }Error:At this point, you cannot really be sure that you have the lock. Fortunately, the haveLock variable takes care of that for you.niRFSG_UnlockSession(vi, &haveLock); return error; } |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Locking

<!--NI_TOPIC bundle=rfsg-c-api-ref path=group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html language=enus -->
## TOPIC 00182: niRFSG_UnlockSession

- bundle_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- source_path: `group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html`
- source_url: https://docs-be.ni.com/bundle/rfsg-c-api-ref/raw/resource/enus/group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga586c699e54f2f35141821d45d126cc5d.html
- document_id: `rfsg-c-api-ref`
- page_type: `leaf`
- content_type: `reference`
- source_description: Releases a lock obtained on an NI-RFSG device session by calling the niRFSG_LockSession function. SyntaxViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_UnlockSession(ViSession vi, ViBoolean *callerHasLock)RemarksSupported Devices: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5654/5654 with PXIe

### niRFSG_UnlockSession

Releases a lock obtained on an NI-RFSG device session by calling the [niRFSG_LockSession](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__locking_1ga3d0cfeb379c0dcb96e194258505aa0c9.html) function.

#### Syntax

ViStatus __stdcall niRFSG_UnlockSession(ViSession vi, ViBoolean *callerHasLock)

#### Remarks

**Supported Devices**: PXI-5610, PXIe-5611, PXIe-5644/5645/5646, PXI/PXIe-5650/5651/5652, PXIe-5654/5654 with PXIe-5696, PXI-5670/5671, PXIe-5672/5673/5673E, PXIe-5820/5840/5841/5842/5860

#### Parameters

| Name | Direction | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| vi | [in] | ViSession | Identifies your instrument session. The ViSession handle is obtained from the niRFSG_Init function or the niRFSG_InitWithOptions function and identifies a particular instrument session. |
| callerHasLock | [out] | ViBoolean * | Keeps track of whether you obtain a lock and therefore need to unlock the session. Pass the address of a local ViBoolean variable. In the declaration of the local variable, initialize it to VI_FALSE. Pass the address of the same local variable to any other calls you make to the niRFSG_LockSession function or the niRFSG_UnlockSession function in the same function.This parameter serves as a convenience. If you do not want to use this parameter, pass VI_NULL.The parameter is an input/output parameter. The niRFSG_LockSession function and the niRFSG_UnlockSession each inspect the current value and take the following actions:If the value is VI_TRUE, the niRFSG_LockSession function does not lock the session again. If the value is VI_FALSE, the niRFSG_LockSession function obtains the lock and sets the value of the parameter to VI_TRUE.If the value is VI_FALSE, the niRFSG_UnlockSession function does not attempt to unlock the session. If the value is VI_TRUE, the niRFSG_UnlockSession function releases the lock and sets the value of the parameter to VI_FALSE.Thus, you can call the niRFSG_UnlockSession function at the end of your function without worrying about whether you have the lock.Example:ViStatus TestFunc (ViSession vi, ViInt32 flags) { ViStatus error = VI_SUCCESS; ViBoolean haveLock = VI_FALSE;if (flags & BIT_1) { viCheckErr( niRFSG_LockSession(vi, &haveLock)); viCheckErr( TakeAction1(vi)); if (flags & BIT_2) { viCheckErr( niRFSG_UnlockSession(vi, &haveLock)); viCheckErr( TakeAction2(vi)); viCheckErr( niRFSG_LockSession(vi, &haveLock)); } if (flags & BIT_3) viCheckErr( TakeAction3(vi)); }Error:At this point, you cannot really be sure that you have the lock. Fortunately, the haveLock variable takes care of that for you.niRFSG_UnlockSession(vi, &haveLock); return error; } |

#### Returns

Returns the status code of this operation. The status code either indicates success or describes an error or warning condition. Examine the status code from each call to an instrument driver function to determine if an error occurred. To obtain a text description of the error code, call the [niRFSG_GetError](group____root__ni_r_f_s_g__functions__utility__error__info_1ga51b799e011460070c57520cdbd64b6f7.html) function. The general meaning of the status code is as follows:

| Value | Meaning |
| --- | --- |
| 0 | Success |
| Positive Values | Warnings |
| Negative Values | Errors |

Parent topic:

Locking
